  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b9e19cdd-01f4-4394-8a9b-cc26f0e46dd8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_2303575520" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2303575520" />
    <a title="Literary Loft" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/78077927-literary-loft"><img alt="Literary Loft" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519225193p2/78077927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2303575520?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Literary Loft" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Literary Loft" href="/user/show/78077927-literary-loft">Literary Loft</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2303575520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15055904000085740032">Oh my goodness! For me, this is the best in Millicent’s Self-Esteem for Busy People series. Why if you ask? Well, while reading it this cold but sunny morning, all of the thoughts and quotes in here spoke to me on a personal level. First of all, it is a sort of a Quote-per-day for 30 days short book and these are some of Millicent’s expressions and wisdom I am eager to share with you so you can be helped with your personal dilemmas and for you to go buy this book now from Amazon online.<br/><br/>1. “Make </span>
  <span id="freeText15055904000085740032" style="display:none">Oh my goodness! For me, this is the best in Millicent’s Self-Esteem for Busy People series. Why if you ask? Well, while reading it this cold but sunny morning, all of the thoughts and quotes in here spoke to me on a personal level. First of all, it is a sort of a Quote-per-day for 30 days short book and these are some of Millicent’s expressions and wisdom I am eager to share with you so you can be helped with your personal dilemmas and for you to go buy this book now from Amazon online.<br /><br />1. “Make yourself necessary to Someone.” Millicent explains that by this, we are always valuable to someone. That our existence always means something to a family member or a friend or even a stranger. That before we contemplate something as tragic as suicide, we must always remember that there are those who find growth in us. That we should know that “everything around us—all our experiences this day—guide our growth (and…others’ growths too.)<br />2. “I have learned silence from the talkative; tolerance from the intolerant and kindness from the unkind.” What I got from this is that we have to learn from the negative traits and experiences of others. Or even ourselves. Look at what those with these traits went through in order to learn from them to better and prepare ourselves for what trouble or tragedy is headed our way.<br />3. “Kindness to others repays us in kindness; respect to others repays us in returned respect. No person in the world ever attempted to wrong another without being injured in—return—some way.” I know this is not an original way of thinking but I’m including it here for you to recognize and relate to so you can feel a connection to Millicent’s book here. It’s a self-explanatory quote isn’t it?<br />4. “Happiness can’t protect us from everything—but it will keep us from doubling our woes when we have those inevitable ‘reverses’.” For me I found this thought to be true. Although happiness is not all serving, it does bar ourselves from getting into a lot of trouble and regret. It is wise to be happy because it comes with benefits to our health and well-being.<br /><br />I recommend this book to that friend of yours or even yourself if you’re going through some personal struggles and low self-esteem. This is the third installment in this self-growth series of Millicent’s. It is short and inspiring and packed with positivity I am sure will make you return to your ambitious, independent, and unbreakable self if you are currently depressed and feeling like your whole world has fallen apart. I, myself have learned some great and valuable tips from it for my own self-growth. I am seeing my faults for the first time and am willing and eager to move past them in order to live a happy and fulfilling life! His advice in here is comforting and inspiring. Get this one and the other three books in this series to get you back on your feet to go out and achieve, attain, and realize all of your dreams and goals! Yay!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15055904000085740032" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FKpBj9czDtK1fJI4IxTiKQT1giV0XxzmBFSDMCjbwme0QEDtT4mnvhJ84eLReZfTfZHEergqQwgM2rOymYCprw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('q4RAMczxCNoka5pmCQbBUhAqPdL1N1QDYf9FLStLwX0LbkFTVEuhtoNr6bz7a7SoaU57jTlCC+1pcXWvmhCqtQ==')})
  }

Her new family descends those steps as well, calling for their Lord to hear their prayers.\n\nPhil Barr begrudgingly knows this, as he cowers in his palatial Hollywood Hills mansion, murderers and thugs auditioning on live TV, sirens ringing in his ears. This wasn’t how his charmed life was supposed to turn out.\n\nAnd DaRWIn knows this best of all, as it predicted the assassination, and the calamitous after-effects some time ago.\n\nOn a certain day, on a certain street in the Middle East, the taking of a single life will mean everything, and it will shake the foundation of humanity. As Chief of Surgical Oncology at Baylor College of Medicine, Dr. Steven Curley has worked with cancer patients for over two decades. While his life\'s work has been to help his patients live longer lives, he found that they helped him in ways he never could have expected. IN MY HANDS is a rare, often emotional look at some of Dr. Curley\'s real patients and real situations in modern cancer care. These stories of resilience, hope, and determination changed and inspired Dr. Curley, and he uses these same stories to encourage patients dealing with the fear and uncertainty coupled with a diagnosis of cancer. Every story in the book has a theme inspired by his patients: Hope, Courage, Strength, Determination, Wonder, Cooperation, Creativity, Diligence, Service, Perseverance, Wisdom, Grace, Consideration, Gratitude, Discernment, Reverence, Resourcefulness, Faith, Beauty, Acceptance, and Empathy. Some are positive messages, reminding us of the importance of maintaining balance between family, work, and leisure activities. Others are examples of the remarkable resilience of the human spirit when facing the reality of and the surgical risks that accompany a cancer diagnosis. Realistically, despite remarkable advances in multidisciplinary cancer care, some remind us cancer is still a potentially lethal and destructive disease affecting patients and the family and friends supporting them. While many people are told that there is no hope in their situation, Dr. Curley\'s patients taught him to always provide hope, to push the envelope and give people a chance, and that hope is a critical component of treatment and care. <span id="freeTextContainer11142355606454920398">I was an early reader of Maxwell Maltz - `Psycho Cybernetics` and that had a definite impact on me. I have read - and actually lectured when I had a large sales organization - on the premises in the book.<br/><br/>I was amazed at the popularity of works such as: The Secret, and The Law of Attraction. I was surprised because they were the same exact principles in the book.<br/><br/>I wrote two books actually based on </span>
  <span id="freeText11142355606454920398" style="display:none">I was an early reader of Maxwell Maltz - `Psycho Cybernetics` and that had a definite impact on me. I have read - and actually lectured when I had a large sales organization - on the premises in the book.<br /><br />I was amazed at the popularity of works such as: The Secret, and The Law of Attraction. I was surprised because they were the same exact principles in the book.<br /><br />I wrote two books actually based on these premises - but they are presented in a light hearted manner - and dispels the belief that they are `new' or `secret'.<br /><br />They are written to be fun read with a chuckle, and yet espouses all the tenets.<br /><br /><br /></span>
